## **A batting cage for sales teams**
Empower your team with actionable conversational strategies that can be easily practiced and utilized in the field.
![](https://cdn.prod.website-files.com/65e867507f77f80a08ba1bd5/6636059381c78be748f5c6ab_Step%201.jpg)
**STEP** 1
Identify a challenging sales situation.
![](https://cdn.prod.website-files.com/65e867507f77f80a08ba1bd5/66360593f5dd1257d85b2d2a_Step%202.jpg)
**STEP** 2
Use Roleplay AI to craft strategic talk tracks for the situation.
![](https://cdn.prod.website-files.com/65e867507f77f80a08ba1bd5/66b4ef0ac0bf46153fd41120_3.jpg)
**STEP 3**
Placing learners in a "Sales Batting Cage" to practice talks and techniques before challenging them with AI to solidify their knowledge.
![](https://cdn.prod.website-files.com/65e867507f77f80a08ba1bd5/66b4ef0ab4f65187a0932346_31.jpg)
**STEP 3.1**
Learners engage in open-ended conversations with Customer AI, mastering techniques and adapting to surprises.

Your team aligns with the message and is ready to face real customers.

Once your team has practiced various conversational strategies, our AI challenges them in an open-ended conversation, helping them master certain techniques and adapt to surprises. 
— Live, unpredictable conversations with AI of various levels of difficulty.  
— Immediate Feedback: Offering learners concise, actionable insights.   
— Managerial Insights: Delivering comprehensive performance reports.

FAQ
## You ask. We answer.
[**General questions**](https://www.practis.ai/#w-tabs-0-data-w-pane-0)[**Learning proccess**](https://www.practis.ai/#w-tabs-0-data-w-pane-1)
What are the key components of the Practis Platform? 
The Practis Platform includes three essential components designed to optimize sales training and performance management. The web portal acts as the foundation of our comprehensive sales training software, allowing team leaders to efficiently manage teams, track learning progress, and conduct content creation and management.
The training app, suitable for all mobile devices, is tailored for trainees to immerse themselves in scenario-based training, practice their skills, complete accuracy tests, and receive essential real-time feedback.
ScrimmageAI is improvisational
The team leader app, a vital extension of the web portal, is available across platforms and allows leaders to review submissions and deliver customizable feedback, enhancing the sales training experience for every team member.
[Watch Now: Explore the Team Leader App in Action](https://vimeo.com/manage/videos/861359391)
How quickly can we start using Practis?
Practis, as a scalable sales training system, allows you to begin training within a matter of days, leveraging its web-based application and mobile compatibility. There's no requirement for additional hardware or software, minimizing initial setup costs. The sales training software streamlines the process of managing and delivering training content, enabling a swift and effective training rollout.
**Can Practis handle training for big teams in different locations?**
Practis is perfectly suited for handling training needs across geographically dispersed teams, offering a consistent and comprehensive training platform that includes virtual sales role-play ability.
Additionally, its flexible licensing options allow you to easily adjust the number of active users to match seasonal demands. This adaptability ensures that Practis can efficiently support any team size, at any time, making it an ideal choice for dynamic business environments.
**What measurable benefits does Practis deliver for sales teams?**
Businesses utilizing Practis can anticipate substantial enhancements in sales performance, marked by increased close rates and improved sales training retention. These outcomes are consistently evidenced in our comprehensive case studies, showcasing Practis's effectiveness in driving measurable improvements in sales metrics.
Case studies
[Green Growth: How Practis Doubled New Hire Retention and Supercharged Sales in Lawn Care](https://cdn.prod.website-files.com/65e867507f77f80a08ba1bd5/665ccb5c902df4f04b843ff2_Green_Growth_Practis_Doubled_New_Hire_Retention_Supercharged_Sales_Lawn_Care.pdf)

What are the content creation options available in Practis?
Practis offers two primary methods for creating training content. The first is the Practis Roleplay AI, an AI-powered tool designed to generate customer interaction scenarios from descriptions of sales situations. The second option is the use of an integrated editor, which allows you to manually create and customize various training materials tailored to your specific needs.
**How does the Practis Roleplay AI enhance content creation for training?**
The Practis Roleplay AI is an AI-based tool specifically designed to assist in the development of sales training content. It simplifies the content creation process by enabling users to generate, edit, and refine training materials through a guided wizard. This wizard asks specific questions about your sales challenges and uses your responses to produce tailored training content.
Once generated, you can further customize this content interactively by engaging with the AI, making it an ideal solution for enhancing customer interaction skills or creating new content from scratch.
**How does Practis make training easier for sales managers?**
Practis makes a manager's job easier by using AI to help put together and improve training materials quickly. Managers can then send out these fresh trainings right away. To see just how simple it is, check out this short video showing the process. Practis also cuts down on work by automating how we check what trainees have learned and making sure everyone’s up to speed.
The system includes Learning Management System (LMS) that helps managers pick out and keep the best trainings to share with any number of team members, no matter where they are. Plus, Practis has an automatic way to remind trainees if they’re behind and let team leaders see who needs to catch up at a glance.
[Practis for team leaders](https://cdn.prod.website-files.com/65e867507f77f80a08ba1bd5/665ccb5c254938203311c5c1_Team-leaders.pdf)
[Practis for learners](https://cdn.prod.website-files.com/65e867507f77f80a08ba1bd5/665ccb5c300eabc991663701_Learners.pdf)
**What is the rationale behind Practis's emphasis on repeated scenario practice?**
Practis prioritizes repeated scenario practice because it solidifies key skills and bolsters memory, especially under the stress of real sales situations. This repetition, combined with modern, engaging training techniques, ensures that sales teams retain information and apply it effectively. Additionally, to maximize learning outcomes, Practis advocates for a diverse mix of training methods, enhancing versatility and adaptability in sales strategies.
**How does Practis tailor training for different expertise levels within a sales team?**
"Practis offers tailored training to effectively elevate the entire spectrum of sales talent within your team. It's not just the top performers who can drive revenue; there's immense value in developing your mid-level sales professionals. In fact, studies have shown _(i think there should be a source of this concept)_ — and as illustrated here — that improving the skills of the mid-level 70% of your sales team can have a more significant impact on total revenue than the same improvement among your top performers. With Practis, you can unlock this potential and see a transformative effect on your sales outcomes.
![Image titled 'The Revenue Catalyst: Improving the 70% in the middle has the biggest impact on aggregate revenues', featuring three bar graphs comparing performance gains among Top, Mid, and Low Performers. The slide indicates that a 5% gain in mid-level performers contributes significantly more to overall revenue than the same gain in top performers, according to the Sales Executive Council.](https://cdn.prod.website-files.com/65e867507f77f80a08ba1bd5/66366c16c40e1c75444e787e_Ed-Keynote-Source.001.jpeg)
**How does Practis track and report on training progress for individuals and teams?**
Practis can handle teams of any size and uses its built-in system to keep track of detailed training progress and performance. Managers get clear reports on how each person and the whole team are doing. Additionally, Practis allows you to create custom reports in Excel format. These reports let you look at training results from different angles, making it easier to understand and improve your team’s training experiences.

### See how Prospeo can help you
![Case Study 1](https://prospeo.io/_next/image?url=%2Fimages%2Fusecase-image1.webp&w=750&q=75)
“We now reach buyers before they even talk to a competitor.”
Felix Frank
Founder at StackOptimise
Sales teams  can build targeted lists in seconds, reach the right decision makers with verified emails and mobile numbers, and book more meetings from the same activity.
Data Reps Can Trust
Give reps verified emails and mobile numbers so they stop fixing lists and focus on booking meetings.
01
Talk to buyers who are in market
Use intent-style filters like buying intent, headcount growth in a specific department, and tech usage to target companies that are actively looking for your type of product, not just anyone in your market.
02
Prospecting that feels easy
Build targeted lists in seconds, export clean data or capture contacts with the extension, then send directly from your sequencer without manual cleanup.
03
Pay only for good data
You only pay for verified emails and mobile numbers, at a fair price, so you can give every rep more leads without blowing up the budget.
04

Tai Shver
Manager of Business Development at Loopio
Outbound agencies  can run cold outbound and lead generation for multiple clients with stable deliverability, better reply rates, and stronger results, while keeping margins healthy.
More replies for your clients
Better data means more opened emails, more positive replies, and more meetings you can show in your reports.
01
Less domain rotation, more time
Clean, verified data keeps bounce rates low, so you spend less time buying new domains, warming inboxes, and repairing reputation for every client.
02
Reach buyers who actually want the offer
Use intent-style filters like buying intent, headcount growth in a specific department, and tech usage to target companies that are actively looking for your type of product, not just anyone in your market.
03
Best data at the best price
You get high-quality, fresh leads data, and pay only for verified emails and mobile numbers, so you can protect your margins while still giving clients strong results.

Gleb Kolyada
Founder at Datazn

Test audiences in a day
Build targeted lists of thousands of contacts in seconds, export verified emails and mobile numbers, and start talking to them the same day.
01
Reach people who actually need your product
Use intent-style filters like buying intent, headcount growth in a specific department, and tech usage to target companies that are actively looking for your product, not just anyone in your market.
02

03

“24% Increase in Meeting Booking Rate”
Henry Clayton
Principal SDR at Allego
RevOps teams can standardize data, protect domains, and give every rep more of the right leads at a clear cost per lead.
Standardize GTM inputs
Give every team the same verified emails and mobile numbers from one source, so performance depends on playbooks and skills, not on who bought which list.
01
Protect deliverability
Verified contacts go through strong checks before they reach your sequences, so bounce rates stay low, domains stay healthy, and campaigns do not stall because of bad lists.
02
Keep ICP lists focused
Combine buying intent, headcount growth in target teams, and tech filters with regular refresh so segments stay close to your real ICP and focus on accounts that are more likely to buy.
03
Clear cost per lead
You only pay for validated and verified contacts, cheaper than other providers, so it is simple to track what each lead costs and how many leads each rep gets.

#  Drive performance with compensation plans 
Maximize the impact of your comp plans. QuotaPath motivates sellers and centralizes sales commission tracking, modeling, and payouts.   
  
Build AI-powered comp plans, automate tracking and payouts, and get audit-ready accuracy.

## Accelerate efficient growth with your comp plans
**80% of revenue leaders** admit their compensation plans fail to align with business goals. Why? Many comp plans incentivize the wrong behaviors or fail to show reps what deals make them—and the business— the most money.
At QuotaPath, we believe the right comp plan doesn’t just reward sales—it shapes business performance.
Optimize plans for revenue growth with QuotaPath’s AI-powered Plan Builder. Upload your compensation plan document to generate a tailored structure, or use our intuitive builder to customize components like quotas, accelerators, and commission rates and optimize for performance. 
Align your plans effortlessly with strategic goals such as increasing average contract value, closing more multi-year contracts, and maximizing customer lifetime value. 
[Learn to Build Comp Plans](https://www.quotapath.com/build-sales-compensation-plans/)
![](data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20viewBox='0%200%201240%201088'%3E%3C/svg%3E)
## Streamline commission management
Save hours (even days) running commissions. 
Set up payout eligibility rules, confidently resolve commission disputes, and ensure accurate payouts through an efficient commission management process. 
Lock previous-period data to preserve audit trails and ensure the right eyes are on each deal at the right time by enabling tailored approval processes for reps, managers, executives, and finance.
**Reduce errors** , **save time,** and **enhance accountability** with transparent, reliable workflows.
[Learn How to Manage Commissions](https://www.quotapath.com/automate-commission-tracking/)
![](data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20viewBox='0%200%20620%20477'%3E%3C/svg%3E)
## Integrate your stack
Simplify your commission process with trusted connected data pulled directly from your CRM, ERP, Accounting, and Data Warehouse systems. Enable a true end-to-end commission cycle with our Rippling integration to fully automate payroll.
With flexible self-service integrations and configurable payout rules, easily adapt your processes as your business evolves.
[View Integrations](https://www.quotapath.com/integrations-hub/)

Functional Functional Always active 
The technical storage or access is strictly necessary for the legitimate purpose of enabling the use of a specific service explicitly requested by the subscriber or user, or for the sole purpose of carrying out the transmission of a communication over an electronic communications network.
Preferences Preferences
The technical storage or access is necessary for the legitimate purpose of storing preferences that are not requested by the subscriber or user.
Statistics Statistics
The technical storage or access that is used exclusively for statistical purposes. The technical storage or access that is used exclusively for anonymous statistical purposes. Without a subpoena, voluntary compliance on the part of your Internet Service Provider, or additional records from a third party, information stored or retrieved for this purpose alone cannot usually be used to identify you.
Marketing Marketing

## Why ReachOwl Is Different From Other Automation Tools
Most Instagram and Facebook automation tools rely on cloud bots, shared IPs, or aggressive behavior that increases the risk of account restrictions. 
ReachOwl works differently.
  * ![features Images](https://reachowl.com/images/new-theme/8.svg)
Runs inside your own browser session
Automation uses your actual Facebook and Instagram login — just like a human. 
  * ![features Images](https://reachowl.com/images/new-theme/9.svg)
Human-like actions and delays
Every action follows realistic limits and timing. 
  * ![features Images](https://reachowl.com/images/new-theme/10.svg)
No cloud bots or shared infrastructure
No API abuse. No detectable automation footprint. 
  * ![features Images](https://reachowl.com/images/new-theme/7.svg)
Works quietly in the background
Launch campaigns once. Keep your browser open. ReachOwl handles the rest. 

Built for long-term outreach, not short-term spam.

FAQ
## Commonly asked questions
By offering concise and informative responses, this section helps users find solutions without the need to contact customer support, saving time 
Will my social media account be safe? 
Yes. ReachOwl works in a very human-like manner by using randomized delays between actions such as messages and friend requests. You can target users using keywords, minimum friend counts, and profile bio filters to reach the right audience. Campaign-level and account-level limits help reduce risk. We recommend using secondary (alt) accounts for best safety. 
Can I get blocked for using ReachOwl? 
It’s unlikely. ReachOwl runs automation directly in your browser as a background process. However, no tool can fully bypass social media platforms’ security systems. For safety, we recommend using ReachOwl with a secondary profile. 
How can I use ReachOwl? 
Simply install the ReachOwl extension from the Chrome Web Store and start using its automation features. 
Do I need an anti-detect browser? 
No. ReachOwl runs directly in your browser. You can add multiple accounts and assign a proxy to each account within ReachOwl—no anti-detect browser is required. 
Is Instagram DM automation safe? 
ReachOwl uses your real browser session and human-like behavior to reduce risk. 
Does this work for Facebook Messenger automation? 
Yes. ReachOwl supports Facebook DM and Messenger-based workflows. 
Do I need proxies or anti-detect browsers? 
No. ReachOwl is designed to work without additional tools.

## Built for the Agentic Era of GTM
From tool sprawl to agent sprawl, GTM needs coordination, not more noise. See Deepinder Singh Dhingra, Founder & CEO of RevSure AI, explain why the future of GTM belongs to coordinated agentic systems.

With RevSure, Jason Beddall’s team gained full-funnel visibility, daily pipeline projections, and AI-driven ROI insights that connected every campaign to revenue impact.

Introducing RevSure Agent Hub
##  AI Agents Purpose-Built for GTM Execution
RevSure Agent Hub brings agentic AI to life for B2B Go-to-Market, an intelligent framework designed to automate and optimize every stage of your GTM motion. From marketing attribution and campaign reallocation to pipeline prediction and next-best actions, our specialized AI agents work across the full funnel to accelerate execution, improve ROI, and increase revenue predictability.

Power Agents with the Right Data
Pull data from queries, APIs, or tools, refine with filters, and enhance decisions with AI-powered intent and custom knowledge.

## Your Complete AI ABM Solution
Powerful ways to grow and engage your whole market
### Inbound Nurture
  * Offer every inbound lead the white glove, VIP treatment to stand out from the competition
  * ICP scoring based on rich research builds immediate confidence with your sales team
  * Reduce friction, time to first-touch and manual processes to 10x your inbound value


#### Plus!
Gather deeper engagement metrics than ever before and keep your CRM 100% clean
### Outbound Education
  * Educate every target prospect on the challenges and benefits you can help them with
  * Wherever they are in their buyer journey, your messages will adjust to their needs
  * Multi-threaded, multi-channel and multi-touch by default for every campaign


#### Plus!
Find and convert partners to grow your channel and spread the word
Taken together? We can augment ABM programmes for every touchpoint in your prospect journey, leaving no stone unturned. Empowering your team to focus on the uniquely human aspect of sales - real conversations based on deep insights.

AI & Natural Language Search Ask anything, find everything - your Rings data responds to plain English and pushes insights to you at critical moments
Track Job Changes Don't miss an opportunity -view and track your network in motion.
Propietary AI Scoring Stop guessing who matters - our AI scores companies, investors, and funds to fast-track your decisions.

## Insights that drive revenue
Diagnose
### Understand why deals are really lost
AI finds and auto-tags the root causes hidden in unstructured data – like product, pricing, timing, or competition – so you know why deals are really lost.

Analyze
### Understand trends and seize opportunities
Drill down into actionable insights and get recommendations to improve your product, pricing, trust, timing, and sales process.

Improve
### Empower your teams to win more – together
Give Sales, Marketing, RevOps, and Product the insights and guidance they need to course-correct, align, and stay ahead of the competition across your ICP tiers.

## Bring lost deals back – smarter, faster, and automatically
Reconnect
### Rebuild interest
Re-engagement workflows put your closed-lost pipeline to work with personalized automation that recovers revenue.

Personalize
### Personalize outreach
Send tailored emails based on loss reasons – so every follow-up speaks directly to the buyer's concerns.

Automate
### Re-engage at the right moment
Trigger follow-ups based on product updates, competitor renewals, or engagement signals – then route deals back to reps with full context.

To provide the best experiences, we use technologies like cookies to store and/or access device information. Consenting to these technologies will allow us to process data such as browsing behavior or unique IDs on this site. Not consenting or withdrawing consent, may adversely affect certain features and functions.
Functional Functional Always active 
The technical storage or access is strictly necessary for the legitimate purpose of enabling the use of a specific service explicitly requested by the subscriber or user, or for the sole purpose of carrying out the transmission of a communication over an electronic communications network.
Preferences Preferences
The technical storage or access is necessary for the legitimate purpose of storing preferences that are not requested by the subscriber or user.
Statistics Statistics
The technical storage or access that is used exclusively for statistical purposes. The technical storage or access that is used exclusively for anonymous statistical purposes. Without a subpoena, voluntary compliance on the part of your Internet Service Provider, or additional records from a third party, information stored or retrieved for this purpose alone cannot usually be used to identify you.
Marketing Marketing
The technical storage or access is required to create user profiles to send advertising, or to track the user on a website or across several websites for similar marketing purposes.

### Powerful Commission Automation
**Ready to become your sales team's hero?**   
  
Sales Cookie is a powerful sales commission management solution for SMBs. Our cloud-based solution makes it easy to [design](https://salescookie.com/Home/Setup) and manage sales incentive plans - even very complex ones. Every sales representative gets a personalized [dashboard](https://salescookie.com/Home/IncentiveDashboards) with their goals, crediting, and rewards. All [calculations](https://salescookie.com/Home/Calculations) are fast and accurate so you can pay reps on time. Here is what the **admin console** and **rep dashboards** look like.

### How It Works
**Four Simple Steps To Automate Your Incentive Program**   
  
Whether you want to keep things simple or require complex plans, we have your back. From multi-currency support to advanced formulas, we're confident we can handle your commission structure. Sales Cookie supports all commission structures - including splits, quotas, ramp ups, formulas, rollups, overrides, caps, and much much more. 
![](https://salescookie.com/Content/Overview/img/step1.png)   

#### Create Incentive Plans
Define sales goals, potential rewards, terms & conditions. 
![](https://salescookie.com/Content/Overview/img/step2.png)   

#### Import Sales Transactions
Sync sales transaction data from your CRM or accounting system. 
![](https://salescookie.com/Content/Overview/img/step3.png)   

#### Run Commission Calculations
Run one-shot calculations across all reps in a few clicks. 
![](https://salescookie.com/Content/Overview/img/step4.png)   

#### Publish To Rep Dashboards
Your reps can access their statements online any time. 
  
  

### Next-Gen Commission Software
**Everything You Need + More**   
  
It's time to say goodbye to sales commission headaches! From [multi-currency](https://salescookie.com/Home/Currencies) support to [enterprise reporting](https://salescookie.com/Home/Reporting), you'll find [features](https://salescookie.com/Home/Pricing#features) you need. Avoid administrative headaches and save time & money. Captivate your sales force and unleash their true potential. 
![](https://salescookie.com/Content/Overview/img/aiEngine.png)
## AI Everywhere
Answer payee questions using AI. Update logic and formulas with AI. Administer commissions through AI queries. 
![](https://salescookie.com/Content/Overview/img/clawback.png)
## Claw-Backs
Query your commission history to automatically [reverse](https://support2.salescookie.com/portal/en/kb/articles/kb-how-can-i-claw-back-commissions) commissions when certain claw-back events occur. 
![](https://salescookie.com/Content/Overview/img/trueup.png)
## True-Ups
Re-process past deals to re-calculate what is owed, and [deduct ](https://support2.salescookie.com/portal/en/kb/articles/kb-how-can-i-deal-with-ever-changing-sales-data) what has been paid before (deltas). 
![](https://salescookie.com/Content/Overview/img/override.jpg)
## Overrides
Easily create team-based and manager [override](https://support2.salescookie.com/portal/en/kb/articles/kb-recipe-how-to-setup-manager-override-plans) plans. We even support complex [crediting logic](https://support2.salescookie.com/portal/en/kb/articles/kb-how-can-i-specify-a-dynamic-crediting-formula-advanced) to pay managers. 
![](https://salescookie.com/Content/Overview/img/doublepayment.png)
## Double-Payment
Sales Cookie automatically detects [double-payments](https://support2.salescookie.com/portal/en/kb/articles/kb-how-can-i-prevent-double-payment-of-commissions). This may happen if deal dates are moved to future periods. 
![](https://salescookie.com/Content/Overview/img/exception.png)
## Exceptions
Define commission exceptions by adding [payout](https://support2.salescookie.com/portal/en/kb/articles/kb-how-can-i-calculate-a-complicated-per-transaction-reward-advanced) or [filtering](https://support2.salescookie.com/portal/en/kb/articles/kb-how-can-i-specify-a-dynamic-transaction-filtering-formula-advanced) logic. Exceptions can be as easy or as complex as you want. 
![](https://salescookie.com/Content/Overview/img/advance.png)
## Advances
Configure automated commission advances and [repayments](https://blog.salescookie.com/2024/07/16/understanding-commission-advances-and-repayments-complete-guide/). Easily track the balance owed by each rep. 
![](https://salescookie.com/Content/Overview/img/delayedRelease.png)
## Delayed Release
Earn commissions when deals close. Pay when you get paid. Reps can view [outstanding](https://support2.salescookie.com/portal/en/kb/articles/kb-how-can-i-show-withheld-commissions-to-my-reps) commissions. Track [liabilities](https://support2.salescookie.com/portal/en/kb/articles/how-can-i-analyze-liabilities). 
![](https://salescookie.com/Content/Overview/img/adjust.png)
## Adjustments
Easily make [adjustments](https://support2.salescookie.com/portal/en/kb/articles/kb-how-can-i-manually-adjust-sales-commissions) to commissions. Adjustments are [preserved](https://support2.salescookie.com/portal/en/kb/articles/kb-are-manual-adjustments-always-preserved-on-re-calculation) when you re-calculate commissions. 
![](https://salescookie.com/Content/Overview/img/crossLookup.png)
## Cross-Lookups
Issue [data queries](https://support2.salescookie.com/portal/en/kb/articles/kb-how-do-advanced-sql-statements-work) spanning multiple data sources. Match records across multiple systems (ex: invoice and deals). 
![](https://salescookie.com/Content/Overview/img/liabilities.png)
## Liability Tracking
Track all [differences](https://support2.salescookie.com/portal/en/kb/articles/how-can-i-analyze-liabilities) between earned and actual commissions. Empower reps to view [pending](https://support2.salescookie.com/portal/en/kb/articles/kb-how-can-i-show-withheld-commissions-to-my-reps) commissions. 
![](https://salescookie.com/Content/Overview/img/queryData.png)
## Complex Queries
Query, join, sort and group [data](https://support2.salescookie.com/portal/en/kb/articles/kb-how-do-advanced-sql-statements-work). Find duplicates. Analyze your sale history to find if a customer is a new or repeat one.

Effortlessly update your CRM fields and Notes using your voice, with no more tedious typing or form-filling. Our intuitive plug-in lets you simply speak your updates, freeing up your time and energy so that you can focus on the Deal. Plus, our plug-in seamlessly integrates with your CRM's customization, ensuring it adapts to your company's unique needs.

#  Say Goodbye to Manual Entries and Embrace the Future of CRM Verbal Updates!
## **Verbal Field Updates**
With SalesTalk’s **Words2Actions** CRM plugin, users can now verbally update their CRM fields from wherever they are working! This one of kind patent pending feature _**adds the easy**_ into your workweek. From your desktop to your smartphone, **Words2Actions** works where you work!
## **Verbal Note Taking**
If you need to jot down a detailed note about a contact or lead after a call or meeting has ended, worry not! Simply click the Create Note button on the **Words2Actions** page to record your Notes that automatically gets added back into your CRM.

##  Salesforce FAQs 
###  What is Salesforce? 
Salesforce is the [**#1 AI CRM**](https://www.salesforce.com/in/crm/worlds-number-one-crm/) (customer relationship management) platform. We bring companies and customers together by providing a unified set of applications — powered by [agentic AI](https://www.salesforce.com/in/agentforce/what-is-agentic-ai/)[ ](https://www.salesforce.com/agentforce/what-is-agentic-ai/)and data — that help every department, including sales, service, marketing, commerce, and IT, work as one. You can learn more about [what Salesforce is](https://www.salesforce.com/in/products/what-is-salesforce/) and [what Salesforce does](https://www.salesforce.com/in/blog/what-does-salesforce-do/) by visiting [our official resources](https://www.salesforce.com/in/company/our-story/). Our cloud-based agentic solutions help you find more leads, close more deals, and provide better service to your customers, all on a single, integrated agentic platform.
###  What is an CRM and why do businesses need one? 
[**CRM**](https://www.salesforce.com/in/crm/what-is-crm/) stands for **customer relationship management.** It’s a technology for managing all your company’s relationships and interactions with customers and potential customers. A CRM system helps you:  
  
**• Organise** contact information, leads, and customer service data  
**• Automate** tasks like logging calls and sending follow-up emails**  
• Analyse** data to understand customer behaviour and business performance  
  
A CRM, especially one powered by AI like Salesforce, is essential for growth because it gives you a**single** , [**360-degree view** of every customer](https://www.salesforce.com/in/blog/what-exactly-is-salesforce-customer-360/), allowing you to build stronger, more profitable relationships at scale.
###  What is agentic AI and how is it used in Salesforce? 
[**Agentic AI**](https://www.salesforce.com/in/agentforce/what-is-agentic-ai/) refers to advanced artificial intelligence systems that can act [**autonomously**](https://www.salesforce.com/in/agentforce/ai-agents/autonomous-agents/) to achieve a specific goal with minimal human intervention. Unlike traditional [AI](https://www.salesforce.com/in/artificial-intelligence/what-is-ai/)[ ](https://www.salesforce.com/artificial-intelligence/what-is-ai/)that only generates content or analyses data, agentic AI can reason, plan multistep actions, and execute tasks.  
  
In Salesforce, agentic AI — part of our [**Agentforce**](https://www.salesforce.com/in/agentforce/) technology — is used to:  
  
**• Automate** complex workflows like lead qualification or service case resolution  
**• Predict** business outcomes, such as which deals are likely to close  
**• Personalise** every customer interaction across marketing, sales, and service channels
###  How does Salesforce CRM help my small business grow? 
Salesforce offers agentic CRM solutions tailored for companies of all sizes, from [startups and small businesses](https://www.salesforce.com/in/small-business/)[ ](https://www.salesforce.com/small-business/)to large global enterprises. Our Agentforce 360 Platform is **flexible** and **scalable** , allowing you to start with the essentials you need — like sales, service, commerce, or marketing — and easily add more functionality as your business grows. This ensures you only pay for what you use and have an [AI and CRM](https://www.salesforce.com/in/crm/ai-crm/) platform that can grow with your business.

#### General Information
We use three kinds of cookies on our websites: required, functional, and advertising. You can choose whether functional and advertising cookies apply. Click on the different cookie categories to find out more about each category and to change the default settings.   
[Privacy Statement](https://www.salesforce.com/company/privacy/full_privacy/)
#### Required Cookies
Always Active
Required cookies are necessary for basic website functionality. Some examples include: session cookies needed to transmit the website, authentication cookies, and security cookies.
Cookies Details‎
#### Functional Cookies
Functional Cookies
Functional cookies enhance functions, performance, and services on the website. Some examples include: cookies used to analyze site traffic, cookies used for market research, and cookies used to display advertising that is not directed to a particular individual.
Cookies Details‎
#### Advertising Cookies
Advertising Cookies
Advertising cookies track activity across websites in order to understand a viewer’s interests, and direct them specific marketing. Some examples include: cookies used for remarketing, or interest-based advertising.
Cookies Details‎

##  Manage All Replies Across Email & LinkedIn With Primebox™
Primebox™ keeps you in control by consolidating all your replies across email and LinkedIn in one place, capturing replies from any address (even if the prospect responds from a different email) and layering in AI analysis and smart tools to help you respond faster, better, and always on time - so you never lose a prospect in the noise. Included for free with every Salesforge subscription.
[Learn more](https://www.salesforge.ai/primebox)
## Never Land In Spam With Free, Unlimited Warm Up
Salesforge comes with free, unlimited access to Warmforge - our email deliverability tool with a premium warm up pool, free of external SMTPs and full of healthy Google Workspace and Microsoft365 mailboxes.  

This pool is used to send emails to and from your mailboxes to establish sender reputation. With Warmforge, you can warm up and monitor the health of all your mailboxes at a glance, without worrying about warm up quality.

## Frequently Asked Questions
If your question’s not down here, message us via the chat!
### What Is Salesforge, And How Does It Stand Out From Other Outreach Tools?
Salesforge is the all-in-one cold outreach platform that combines AI, human workflows, and world-class infrastructure. Unlike other tools, Salesforge lets you run multi-channel campaigns (email + LinkedIn) from a single dashboard, with unlimited mailboxes & LinkedIn senders, built-in AI personalization, deliverability protection, and autonomous AI SDRs.
### What Is Agent Frank & How Does It Work?
Agent Frank is our AI Sales Development Representative (AI SDR). He finds prospects, writes tailored outreach, follows up, and books meetings. With multi-channel enabled, Agent Frank engages prospects on both email and LinkedIn, ensuring your outreach feels natural and human - while freeing up your sales team to focus on closing.
### How Can I Get Started And Is There A Free Trial?
You can get started with Salesforge by clicking here to[ sign up or start your 14-day free trial](https://app.salesforge.ai/signup). To get started with Agent Frank you need to first [book a demo with our team](https://meetings-eu1.hubspot.com/franksondors/ai-agent).
### Do I Have To Use Agent Frank To Run Multi-Channel Campaigns?
Not at all. You can run human-led campaigns only, AI-led campaigns only, or a blend of both. Salesforge was built to give you flexibility, so you can decide when and where AI makes the most impact in your process.
### How Does Salesforge Ensure High Deliverability Across Channels?
Cold outreach falls apart if your messages don’t land. That’s why Salesforge includes features like unlimited warm-up ([powered by Warmforge](https://www.warmforge.ai)), mailbox rotation and more so your emails reach the primary inbox. On LinkedIn, we handle safe sending volumes and scheduling so your account stays compliant.
### Is Email Infrastructure Included?
While you can connect unlimited mailboxes to your Salesforge workspaces, you need to purchase domains and mailboxes separately. Within The Forge Stack we offer 3 infrastructure options: Mailforge (shared infrastructure), Infraforge (private infrastructure) and Primeforge (Google & Microsoft infrastructure). You can also connect your own mailboxes. For more information visit [our email infrastructure page](https://www.salesforge.ai/email-infrastructure).
### Will Salesforge Integrate With My Current Stack?
Salesforge connects with the tools you already use, from Slack and Salesforce to Clay and HubSpot. You can also plug in via Zapier, webhooks or Salesforge API to connect virtually any app. That means your multi-channel outreach fits directly into your existing workflow. You can [browse all integrations here](https://www.salesforge.ai/integrations).
